  2538. # [15:27] <gcp> The injected-class-name of a class (clause
  2539. # [15:27] <gcp> 9
  2540. # [15:27] <gcp> ) is also considered to be a member of that class for the purposes of name
  2541. # [15:27] <gcp> hiding and lookup.
  2542. # [15:27] * Quits: Mnyromyr (MnyroWork@moz-E2E3FF3D.tal.de) (Input/output error)
  2543. # [15:28] <gcp> Section 9, point 2
  2544. # [15:28] <gcp> The
  2545. # [15:28] <gcp> class-
  2546. # [15:28] <gcp> name
  2547. # [15:28] <gcp> is also inserted into the scope of the class itself; this is known as the
  2548. # [15:28] <gcp> injected-class-name
  2549. # [15:28] <gcp> . For purposes of access
  2550. # [15:28] <gcp> checking, the injected-class-name is treated as if it were a public member name
